## Sub 4 Milers

Previously NUTS has updated a [register](https://nuts.org.uk/sub-4/index.htm) of sub 4 milers. This has not been updated since May 2022.
This table is a mirror of that database plus subsequent sub 4 performances that are listed on [World Athletics](https://worldathletics.org/records/toplists/middle-long/one-mile/outdoor/men/senior/2023).
